* the puzzle in the lower-right entrance 1 causes unown r, s, t, u, and v to appear.
* the puzzle in the upper-left entrance 1 causes unown w, x, y, and z to appear.
* the puzzle in the lower-left entrance 1 causes unown k, l, m, n, o, p, and q to appear.

==water world==
[[file:ultra space wilds water world.png|thumb|water world]]
'''ultra space wilds (water world)''' (japanese: '''ã¦ã«ãã©ã¹ãã¼ã¹ã¼ã­ï¼{{tt|æ°´|ã¿ã}}ã®{{tt|ä¸ç|ããã}}ï¼''' ''ultra space zero (water world)'') can be reached through blue warp holes. when a legendary pokã©mon is encountered in this area, its silhouette is first seen above the player behind a waterfall.

===geography===
the water world features a path bordered by rocks in a cave-like area filled with water. plenty of waterfalls surround the area. the pathway leads from the blue warp hole to where the pokã©mon is located as a water splash on the floor surface.

===items===
====dropped after ambush encounters====
sometimes, after a pokã©mon from a water splash is defeated or caught, it will drop an item.

==cave world==
[[file:ultra space wilds cave world.png|thumb|cave world]]
'''ultra space wilds (cave world)''' (japanese: '''ã¦ã«ãã©ã¹ãã¼ã¹ã¼ã­ï¼{{tt|æ´çª|ã©ããã¤}}ã®{{tt|ä¸ç|ããã}}ï¼''' ''ultra space zero (cave world)'') can be reached through yellow warp holes. when a legendary pokã©mon is encountered in this area, its silhouette is first seen in a cave entryway above the player.

===geography===
the cave world features a path surrounded by large cave walls sloped towards an area seemingly seeped with light. the pathway leads from the yellow warp hole to where the pokã©mon is located as a dirt cloud on the ground surface. 

===items===
====dropped after ambush encounters====
sometimes, after a pokã©mon from a dirt cloud is defeated or caught, it will drop an item.
{{itlisth|cave}}
